	k_livonia = {
		color = { 110 80 168 }
			
		capital = c_vidzeme # Riga

		#Titular: created by decision.
		
		ai_primary_priority = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					culture = culture:latgalian
				}
				add = @correct_culture_primary_score
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						culture = culture:latgalian
					}
					culture = { has_cultural_pillar = heritage_baltic }
				}
				add = @better_than_the_alternatives_score
			}
		}

k_albania = {
	color = { 149 45 102 }
	capital = c_dyrrachion # Durrës
	
	can_create = {
		trigger_if = {
			limit = {
				is_ai = yes
			}
			OR = {
				has_title = title:k_naples
				has_title = title:k_sicily
				culture = culture:arberian
			}
		}
	}
	ai_primary_priority = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				culture = culture:arberian
			}
			add = @correct_culture_primary_score
		}
	}
